Page 463 

019581,003487:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
019582,003488: 
019583,003489:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
019584,003490:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
019585,003491:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
019586,003492:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
019587,003493: 
019588,003494:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019589,003495:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.      1) BY ENDIDLE
019590,003496:                                                                                                  #                2) BY NVSUBUSY
019591,003497:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
019592,003498:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019593,003499:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
019594,003500:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
019595,003501: 
019596,003502:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
019597,003503:                                                                                                  #                        CAF             V/N
019598,003504:                                                                                                  #        L               TC              NVSUB
019599,003505:                                                                                                  #        L+1             RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
019600,003506:                                                                                                  #        L+2             RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
019601,003507: 
019602,003508:                                                                                                  #  A ROUTINE CALLED NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL) TO PUT
019603,003509:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019604,003510:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
019605,003511:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019606,003512:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019607,003513: 
019608,003514:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
019609,003515:                                                                                                  #        CAF     WAKEFCADR
019610,003516:                                                                                                  #        TC      NVSUBUSY
019611,003517: 
019612,003518: 
019613,003519:                                                                                                  #  .
019614,003520: 
019615,003521:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
019616,003522:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
019617,003523:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
019618,003524:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
019619,003525: 
019620,003526:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019621,003527:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
019622,003528:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
019623,003529:                                                                                                  #  1)    DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
019624,003530:                                                                                                  #        IS EXCEEDED.
019625,003531:                                                                                                  #  2)    CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 464 

019627,003533:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
019628,003534: 
019629,003535:    4437           44444        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
019630,003536:    4440           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF (LOC
019631,003537:    4441           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
019632,003538:    4442           04635        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
019633,003539:    4443           10647                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
019634,003540:    4444           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
019635,003541: 
019636,003542:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
019637,003543:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
019638,003544: 
019639,003545: 04,2647                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
019640,003546: 04,2647                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019641,003547: 04,2647           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
019642,003548: 04,2650           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
019643,003549: 04,2651           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
019644,003550: 04,2652           04374                           TC       RELDSPON                              
019645,003551: 04,2653           30001                           CA       L                                     
019646,003552: 04,2654           55043                           TS       DSPLIST                               
019647,003553: 04,2655           05133        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
019648,003554: 
019649,003555:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
019650,003556:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
019651,003557:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
019652,003558:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
019653,003559:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
019654,003560: 
019655,003561:    4445                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
019656,003562:    4445                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019657,003563:    4445           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
019658,003564:    4446           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
019659,003565:    4447           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019660,003566:    4450           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
019661,003567:    4451           61012                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
019662,003568:    4452           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019663,003569:    4453           14455                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
019664,003570:    4454           14164                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
019665,003571:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
019666,003572:    4455           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2. PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
019667,003573:    4456           14437                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
019668,003574: 
019669,003575:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
019670,003576:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
019671,003577:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.
019672,003578: 
019673,003579:    4457           56002        RELDSP             XCH      Q                                     #  SET DSPLOCK TO +0, TURN RELDSP LIGHT
019674,003580:    4460           54144                           TS       RELRET                                #  OFF, SEARCH DSPLIST
019675,003581:    4461           44736                           CS       BIT14

Page 465 

019677,003583:    4462           00004                           INHINT                                         
019678,003584:    4463           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              
019679,003585:    4464           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
019680,003586:    4465           11043                           CCS      DSPLIST                               
019681,003587:    4466           04470                           TC       +2                                    
019682,003588:    4467           04473                           TC       RELDSP2                               #  LIST EMPTY
019683,003589:    4470           34755                           CAF      ZERO                                  
019684,003590:    4471           57043                           XCH      DSPLIST                               
019685,003591:    4472           05137                           TC       JOBWAKE                               
019686,003592:    4473           00003        RELDSP2            RELINT                                         
019687,003593:    4474           44747                           CS       BIT5                                  #  TURN OFF KEY RELEASE LIGHT
019688,003594:    4475           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  (BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11)
019689,003595:    4476           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              
019690,003596:    4477           34755                           CAF      ZERO                                  
019691,003597:    4500           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               
019692,003598:    4501           00144                           TC       RELRET                                
019693,003599:    4502           56002        RELDSP1            XCH      Q                                     #  SET DSPLOCK TO +0. NO DSPLIST SEARCH.
019694,003600:    4503           54144                           TS       RELRET                                #  TURN KEY RLSE LIGHT OFF IF DSPLIST IS
019695,003601:                                                                                                  #  EMPTY. LEAVE KEY RLSE LIGHT ALONE IF

019817,003723:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF,
019818,003724:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
019819,003725:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
019820,003726:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
019821,003727:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY, RESTART.
019822,003728:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
019823,003729:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
